48a2(mdo): no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' shes rab kyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpas de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes ma gtogs par sangs
48a3(mdo): rgyas kyi chos gang yang yang dag pa'i shes rab kyis ma mthong ba dang / mngon du ma byas pa dang / khong du ma chung ba de dag med do// de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' rlab kyi stobs phun
48a4(mdo): sum tshogs pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' 'khor gyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor tshul khrims nyams pa ma yin//
48a5(mdo): lta ba nyams pa ma yin/ cho ga nyams pa ma yin/ 'tsho ba nyams pa ma yin gyi/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor ni byang chub sems dpa' mtshungs par spyod pa rnams nyid yin te//
48a6(mdo): de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' 'khor gyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' rdzu 'phrul gyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub
48a7(mdo): sems dpa' 'jig rten pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi yul thams cad dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi rdzu 'phrul gyi yul thams cad zil gyis gnon te/ de yang rdzu 'phrul gyi sangs
48a8(mdo): 'byed pas mcho ga gi zim gyis bzhin to// de 'dodon 'das du'i thing sa can ma gcig gi rtse mam 'dzin no// de shin du zing ba pa dang / slong gi 'jig rten gyi khams dang /
48b1(mdo): dang / nga gsum byan can par 'jag rten gyi khams kya de badzin na/ 'dod na pad+ma'i klung gi skyem srid kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rdul za pa gcigs mas/
48b2(mdo): de zhin du gad+ha'i klung gnyis kyi byem song dang / gsum pa dang / bzhi dang / lnga pA dang / bcu pa dang / zhi shu dang / sum bcu dang / bzhi bcu dang / lnga bcu nas/
48b3(mdo): brjod du med pa'i ming brjod du med pa'i gang+gA'i klung gi byem seng kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rdul tha rab gcig le 'jog kyang / rdul phra rab de la gang ba dang / rdib yang
48b4(mdo): mi mngon te/ 'jig rten gyi khams de rnams kyang phan tshun du gasngo bar mi 'gyur/ sems can de rnams la gnod par yang mi 'gyur te/ de skar na byang chub sems dpa'
48b5(mdo): 'phrul gyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dbang gi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' 'dod na/
48b6(mdo): stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che sna bdun gyis gang bar byin gyis rlob bo// de 'dod na brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i 'jig
48b7(mdo): rten gyi khams kyi bar du rin po che rnam pa sna tshogs kyis/ yongs su gang bar byin gyis brlab ste/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dbang gi sebs phun sum chos
48b8(mdo): ba yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med
49a1(mdo): pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing dag na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ji snyed cig don tha dad ba dang / tshig dang yi ge tha dad pa dang / brjod pa
49a2(mdo): dad pa dang / tshul tha dad pa'i bshad pa de dag byang chub sems dpa'/ skad cig yud tsam thang cig gcig la/ thams cad 'dzin par byed/ khong du chung bar byed//
49a3(mdo): sdom par byed de/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' rnam par mi 'khrugs pa'i byin gyis

49a5(mdo): brlabs byin du brlabs pa la/ gang rnam par 'khrugs par byed pa'i sems can de lta bu sems can gyi ris na med de/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' rnam par mi 'khrug
49a6(mdo): ba'i byin gyis brlabs kyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin no// rigs kyi bu ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' bka' mi gcig pa'i spobs phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/
49a7(mdo): thabs mkhas pa ma gtogs par/ gang byang chub sems dpa'i bka' mi gcig pa'i sems can de lta bu sems can gyi 'is na ma mthong ste/ rigs kyi bu de ltar na/
49a8(mdo): byang chub sems dpa' bka' migacig pa'i skangs phran su ma tshogs pa yin no// rigs kyi bugyis su po de dag dang ldan na byang chub sems dpa' gangs bran pas
49b1(mdo): parnam pa yin na/ rdzogs kyi bu chos su drang ldan na/ byang chub sems dpa' ma shes kun sum chags pa nam yin no// bcu ga na dI swA /
49b2(mdo): la bdag med pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ chos la bdag med pa'i ye shes bus sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ nyi tshe ma yin pa'i mi shes phun sum
49b3(mdo): tshogs pa yin/ ting nge 'dzin gyi snod yul gyi ye shes phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ byin gyi brlabs kyi ye shes phun sram tshogs pa rnams yin/ mi 'dra

49b7(mdo): rigs kyi bu 'di la byang chub sems dpas phung po rnams skye ba yang dag par mthong ngo 'jigs pa dang / 'gog pa yang yang dag par mthong ngo // des phung po skye ba

50a1(mdo): snyam du phung po 'di dag ni bdag med pa sems can med pa/ srog med pa/ gso ba med pa/ gang zag med pa yin mod kyi 'on kyang byis pas
50a2(mdo): se'i skye bo bdag tu 'dzin pa la mngon par zhen pa 'di dag ni 'di ltar bdag cag gi phung po rnams ni bdag cago// bdag cag gi phung po rnams la bdag yod do// bdag cag

50a4(mdo): de khon nyid khong du ma chud pas mgal me'i 'khor lo ltar 'khor bcwa wa khyam mo sasu du sems shing / dethams cad kyang byang chub sems dpas yang dag pa de bzhin du rab tu

50a7(mdo): blo bran du byung ba'i chos la kun brtags pa'i ming gdags te/ sa de yang ro 'dra ba nyid ma yin/ yi ge de dag par ngo ngotshang ma yin mod kyi/ 'di ni ming tsam dang /
50a8(mdo): sa yo du bya/ 'di la mngon par zhen par mi bya'o// khro drar du byung ba'i chos de sa thams cad kyi thams cad gyi du med pa ma yin te/ gzhan gyi rkyen dang /
50b1(mdo): sa spong ba dang / gzhan mazhin rnams kyis 'byung zhing / rkyen dang bral na 'gag pa'i chos 'dri ni yang na// skyes de thams rgyung dru rgyu sems da sru
50b2(mdo): da pa ma pa bzhin du ra ba tu shes te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa 'a chos badrug med pa ma skyes blan sum tshogs pa yin no// de lta na byang chub sems
50b3(mdo): sa man ze ma shes sun sa mtshom na zhe na/ 'dril byang chub sems dpa' nyir rtsala'i m-i shes gang cig pa'i yul 'jug pa / gang cig

50b5(mdo): cheb ma min pa'i ye shes bu na su mtshogs pa yin no// ji wAr na byang chub sems dpa' ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul gyi ye shes sun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ 'di la bya
50b6(mdo): chub sems dpas nyan thos kyi ting nge 'dzin rnams kyang rab tu shes/ rang sangs rgyas ting nge 'dzin rnams kyang rab tu shes/ byang chub sems dpa'i ting 'dzin rnams kyang
50b7(mdo): rab tu shes/ de bzhin gshegs pa'o ting nge 'dzin rnams kyang rab tu shes so// nges ting nge 'dzin gang dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul gang la nyan thos sbyong ba des

54b7(mdo): gnol bar rgyu ba yin no// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang dge ba'i chos la gzhol zhing dge ba'i gyi phyir rgyu ba yin te/ de ltar na byang chub sems
54b8(mdo): dpa' dge ba'i chos la gzhol ba yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dkar po'i chos thams cad bsred pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dperan
55a1(mdo): chu ni rtswa dang / shing gel ba dang / rtsi dang nags tshal thams cad bskyed de// skyes pa rnams kyang phyir zhing rgyas par byed do// de bzhin du byang chub
55a2(mdo): sems dpa' yang ting nge 'dzin gyi chus byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos thams cad rnam par bsgreng ngo // skyes pa rnams kyang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi shing du gyur gyi bar
55a3(mdo): du phyir zhing rgyas par byed do// thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi shing du gyur pa dag gis sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi 'bras bu rnam pa sna tshogs dag gis sems can rnams
55a4(mdo): 'tshe bar 'gyur te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dkar po'i chos thams cad bskyed pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dga' ba dang / dngang pa dang /
55a5(mdo): rangs pa'i gsher ba can yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ chu ni ni ngo bo nyid kyis gsher bar byed do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang ngo bo
55a6(mdo): byed kyis dga' ba dang / rangs pa'i gsher ba can yin te/ sems can gzhan yang dga' ba dang / dang ba dang / rangs pa'i gsher ba can du byed
55a7(mdo): de la dga' ba ni bu'i garten las 'das pa'i chos tshol bam// ngang pa ni sangs rgyas dang / chos dang / dge 'dun la rten pa'o// ras
55a8(mdo): bani gang sems dag brtse/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dga' ba dang / rang pa dang / rangs pa'i gsher dran yin no// ji ltar na byang chub
55b1(mdo): sems dpa' can mongs pa'i rtsa ba'i rgyun thabs cad srung ba yin ne na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ chu ni shIng gi rnam pa dang / rtswa'i rnam pa'i rtsa
55b2(mdo): ngag gi/ rgyan rnams rnams srung lo// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang bsgom pa la gnas pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi chus nyon mongs pa'i rtsa ba'i rgyun thams
55b3(mdo): drang sprul te/ ji ltar nyon mongs pa'i rdza ba'i rgyun 'di dag gi ming yang mi shes pa dang / nyon mongs pa'i dring ba'i bag chags kyang med par 'gyur ba de la
55b4(mdo): bur sbrel te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa'i rtsa ba'i rgyun thams cad rdul te ba yin no// ji ltar nA dang zhing rdeg pa med de gsal ba med
55b5(mdo): zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na chu ni rang bzhin gyis dang zhing rnyog pa med de gsal lo// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang rang bzhin gyis dang
55b6(mdo): zhing rnyog pa med de gsal ba yin no// de la bag la nyal ba dang kun nas ldang ba dang bral bas na dang ba'o// 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang / ga
55b7(mdo): mug dang bralnga bus na rnag pa med pa'o// dbang po rab tu dade bas me gsal bste/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dang zhing rlog pa zed du
55b8(mdo): gsal ba yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa'i yongs su gdung ba rab tu zhibar byed ce na/ rigs bu 'di ste dper na tshun
56a1(mdo): sa chen po dpyid kyi tshabs gdungs pa dang / de las gzhan yang sems can rnams dpyid kyi cha bas gdungs pa rnams rab tu zhi bar
56a2(mdo): byed do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang nyon mongs pas gdungs pa'i sems can gyi khams thams cad chos kyi chus rab tu zhi bar byed de/ de ltar
56a3(mdo): na byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pas yongs su gdungs pa rab tu zhi bar byed pa'o// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' 'dod pa la sred pa bzlog pa yin zhe na/
56a4(mdo): rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na chu yi som pas nyen pa'i sems can rnams kyi sgom pa rnam par bzlog go// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang yul la
56a5(mdo): sreng pas nyen pa'i sems can nyen par gyur pa dag la gang gis sems can de dag gi yul la sred pa ldog par 'gyur ba de lta bu'i chos kyi char mngon par 'bebs
56a6(mdo): te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' 'dod pa la sred pa bzlog par byed do// ji lta ma na byang chub sems dpa' zab cing gting dpag dka' ba yin zhe na/
56a7(mdo): rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ chu yi 'dzings ni zab cing gting dpag dka' ba yin no// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' ye shes yang dag par
56a8(mdo): grub pa yang 'di lta ste/ bdud thams cad dang / mu stegs can thams cad kyis gting dpag dka' zhing zab pa yin te/ de ltar na byang chub sems
56b1(mdo): dpa' ba bcing gting dpag dka' ba yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mtho man 'gengs pa rnams yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'dril ba na/
56b2(mdo): chume krung ni sa'i phyogs mthon dman 'gengs so// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang chos kyi chu yi klung gis sems can gyi kham sna mthon mun 'dangs
56b3(mdo): / de ltar nas 'gengs pa sngar sems can la gnod par byed po de ltar bu byang chub sems dpalam yin gyi/ sems can de rnams la steng brtse ba'i phreng chos
56b4(mdo): kye chu yi klung 'bebs shing / de dag la gnod par mi byed // de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mthon dman 'gengs pa yin no// ji skar na byang chub
56b5(mdo): sems dpe' nyon mongs pa'i rdul thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ chus ni sa'i grogs snyam zhing rdul yu
56b6(mdo): ba thams cad sdum par byed cing rdul de dag zhi bar byed do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang sems can sems brtsub pa rnams 'di lta ste shes rab
56b7(mdo): la gnas pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi chus sems snum par byed cing sems can de dag gi nyon mongs pa'i rdul thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed do// de ltar na byang chub
56b8(mdo): sems dpa' nyon mongs pa'i rdul thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed pa yin no// rigs kyi bu mi tshes bcu po de dag ldan na byang chub sems dpa' chu dang
57a1(mdo): chungs pa rnams yin no// rigs kyi chos bcu dang ldan na/ byang chub sems dpa' me dang mtshungs pa rnams yin no// bcu gang
57a2(mdo): zhe na 'di lta ste/ nyon mongs pa'i phyag dar khrod pa thams cad sreg par byed/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams kyang yongs su smin par byed/ nyon mongs pa'i 'dam
57a3(mdo): thams cad kyang snyam par byed/ me'i phung po dang 'dra ba rnams yin/ spang bar gyur pa rnams yin/ skrag par byed pa rnams yin/ dbugs 'byin pa rnams
57a4(mdo): yin/ sems can thams cad kyi thun mong du gyur pa rnams yin/ mchod par byed pa rnams yin/ mi brnyas par byed pa rnams yin/ rigs kyi bu de la
57a5(mdo): ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa'i phyag dar khung thams cad sreg ce na rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na me ni phyag dar khrod dang rtswa dang / shing
57a6(mdo): dang / gel ba dang / rtsi dang / sdong po thams cad sreg go// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang shes rab kyis bag la nyal ba dang / kun
57a7(mdo): nas ldang ba dang / 'dod chags dang / ne sdang dang / gti mug gi nyon mongs pa'i phyag dar khung thams cad theg ste/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa
57a8(mdo): nyon mongs pa'i phyag dar khung thams cad sreg pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yongs su smin par byed ce na/
57b1(mdo): mtsho 'a /
57b2(mdo): rigs kyi bu 'di lta sa dper na me ni le tog dang / rdzi dang spong ba'i rnam pa thams cad yongs su smin par byed/ de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang shes
57b3(mdo): sa nang gi sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams yis su smin par byed pa'ang ji ltar 'jig par mi 'gyur ba de ltar yongs su smin par byed do// de ltar na sangs rgyas kyi// ji ltar
57b4(mdo): na byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa'i 'dam thams cad snyam par byed ce na/ rigs kyi bu 'di ltar ste/ dper na me ni chu zan gyi 'jam thams cad sam par byed
57b5(mdo): de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang shes rab kyis zag pa can mongs pa'i 'dam thams cad sam par byed de/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa'
57b6(mdo): mongs pa'i 'jam thams cad snyam par byed do// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' me'i phung po dang 'dra ba yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na//
57b7(mdo): sems can zang ba'i nad kyis nyen pa rnams kyi grang ba med par bya ba'i phyir me'i phung po byed do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang nyon mongs pa'i zang
57b8(mdo): ba'i nad kyis btab pa'i sems can rnams kyi nyon mongs pa'i grang nad med par bya ba'i phyir shes rab kyis rab tu dro bar byed de// de ltar na byang chub sems
57b9(mdo): dpa' me'i phung po dang 'dra ba yin no// de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' snang bar gyur pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lnga ste dper na gangs kyi rtse mo 'am//
58a1(mdo): ri 'bigs byed kyi rtse mon me'i phung po chen po 'bar ba des dpag tshad gcig kho ra khor yug tu snang bar byed/ dpag tshad gnyis kho ra khor yug dang /
58a2(mdo): dpag tshad gsum khor khor yug tu yang snang bar byed do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang ye shes kyi snang bas dpag tshad brgyar yang khyab par byed/ dpag tshad srong
58a3(mdo): du'ang khyad par byed/ dpag chang srong phrag brgyar yang khyab par byed pa nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams dpag tu med grangs med pa'i bar du yang khyab par byas nas/ sems can
58a4(mdo): thams cad la ye shes kyis sdang bar byed de/ ye shes kyi snang ba des mi shes pa'i mun pa mun nag thams cad rnam par sel te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' snang bar gyur pa
58a5(mdo): yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' skrag par byed pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na ri dgas kyi rgyal po khro bos me'i phung po chen po mthong na skrag cing dngang la
58a6(mdo): dang nga bar gyur cing / 'di wa rtse mo'i 'jigs pas skrag pas gnas de ring bas kyang shin du ring bar spang ngo // de bzhin du bdud rnams sam/ bdud rtsi ris kyi lha rnams
58a7(mdo): gyis byang chub sems dpa' mthong na skrag cing dngang la dngang bar gyur cing / 'dis sre gzhi brjid chung ba'i phyir gang du byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ming yang mi thosan
58a8(mdo): thong ba sa'i thos gang gi dgas pa ring bas shin du ring bang sa'i phyogs rje yongs su spong // de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' skrag par byed pa yin no// ji lta
58b1(mdo): nga chub mas dpa' brags 'byin pa ni sbyin zhen/ rigs kyi bu 'di la rtse 'aper na mi la la zhig 'brog dgon par 'khyams pa las mo'i phung po mamadza /
58b2(mdo): rdo tsha lasags su song ba dang / des de grong ngas rje'u brang mthong nas de shugs byin de rab tu dadzugs byin nas/ 'jigs pa thams cad dang bral bar 'gyur ro//
58b3(mdo): de shin du byang chub sems dpa' yang 'khor ba'i 'brog dgon par 'khyams pa'i sems can rnams kyis byang chub sems dpa' mthong na/ shugs kyi
58b4(mdo): 'gyur rab tu dbugs byin par 'gyur/ nyon mongs pa'i 'jigs pa thams cad dang bral bar 'gyur te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dbugs 'byin pa
58b5(mdo): min no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems can thams cad kyi thun mong du gyur pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na me ni sems can thams cad
58b6(mdo): kyi mthun mong du gyur ba ste/ ji ltar na rgyal po la phan par nye bar gnas pa ltar gdol bu la yang de bzhin no// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang sem
58b7(mdo): can thams cad mo thun mong du gyur pa yin te/ ji ltar rgyal po la phan pa nye bar gnas pa ltar gdol bu la yang de bzhin te/ de ltar na byang chub sems
58b8(mdo): dpa' sems can thams can dang thun mong du gyur pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mchod par bya ba yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na me
59a1(mdo): la ni bram ze dang / rgyal rigs dang / zong ngal rtsi mi dang / yul gyi mi rnams kyis mchod ngo // de bzhin du byang chub
59a2(mdo): sems dpa' 'ang 'di lta ste/ lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis ston par 'du shes pas mchod de/ de ltar na byang chub
59a3(mdo): sems dpa' mchod par bya ba yin no// ji ltar na mi brnyas pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ me stag chung ngu yang tshig pa'i bdag nyid yin pas
59a4(mdo): ni mi brnyas pa yin no// de bzhin du mos pas spyod pa la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' mthu stobs ma rnyed pa theg pa chen po la las dang po pa yang lha dang /
59a5(mdo): mi dang lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis mi brnyas pa yin no// ngo ci'i phyir zhe na/ lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin rnams
59a6(mdo): kyis byang chub sems dpa' 'di ring por mi thogs par byang chub kyi snying po la 'dug ste/ blan meng pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs pa
59a7(mdo): 'chang rgya bar khong du chud de/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mi brnyas pa yin no// rigs kyi bu chos bcu po de dag dang ldan na byang chub sems dpa' me dpa/
59a8(mdo): mtshungs pa rnams yin no// rigs kyi bu chos bcu ba dang ldan na byang chub sems dpa' rlung dmar dang mtshungs pa rnams yin no// bcu gang zhen 'di
59b1(mdo): kyang byung / da yul kun su sa myed pa dang / sems can rgyal gyis sems pa ma 'as lnga rab tu nal
59b2(mdo): chos kyi char srin chen po kun nas bsgreng ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa'i gdung ba rab tu zhi bar byed pa dang / sems can thams cad ma tsham

59b4(mdo): chos rnams pa tha dad pa'i gzhal med khang chen pa'i bkod ba rnam par dbye ba thams cad rnam par 'byed cing yongs su 'gong ba dang / 'khor gyi dkyil rab
59b5(mdo): bsams kyi shing las shin tu byung ba'i chos kyi gtam yang dag par rnam par nges pa'i me shog yid du 'ong ba'i char rtag tu mngon pa 'bebs pa dang / bsal
59b6(mdo): blangs med par dkar po'i dkyil 'khor yongs su brtsegs pa'i ting dzin dang / rnams byar thar pa dang / gzungs kyi ni rgya mtsho ri rang dang / 'od dang / rnadang

60a1(mdo): 'khor rab tu gtong ba'i phyir ro// rigs kyi bu de ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' gnas med par sbyong ba yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/

60a4(mdo): mi gnas pa yin te/ phung po dang / khams dang / skye mched rnams dang / gzugs dang / tshor ba dang / 'du shes dang / 'du byed dang / rnam par shes

60a7(mdo): par shes pa'i khams dang / lus kyi khams dang / reg bya'i khams dang / lus kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams dang / yid kyi khams dang / chos kyi khams
60a8(mdo): ra yid gyi rnam par shes pa'i khams dang / mig gi skye mched dang / gzugs kyi bu na dang / rna ba'i se mchen dang / rtswa'i bye mched dang / ma
60b1(mdo): rje ma mched dang / lcem skyem tshad dang / ral bye mched dang / lus kyi skye mched dang / reg bya'i skye mched dang / snying kyi skyem ched dang /

60b3(mdo): zang dang / 'khor los sbyar ba dang / brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig chen skye bdag tu 'gyur ba dang / dbang phyug chen po dag tu 'gyur ba dang /

61b4(mdo): bstan pa dang / chos bstan pas nga rgyal nus par byed cing / dge ba drim snyed pas sbyor byed de/ de skar na byang chub sems dpa' se sma rgyal
61b5(mdo): sems pa'i rtse mo 'amar zhing 'jig la rab tu spel bar byed pa ma na// rigs kyi bu ri sna na byang chub sems dpa' tshas pa par sprin chen po kun nas
61b6(mdo): ba yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rlung dmar ni phyogs bzhi nas/ sprin gyi dkyil 'khor kha dog sa tshogs can dang /
61b7(mdo): mtshan zhing 'jam pa'i 'brug sgra rgya mtsho'i dbyangs cani kA re sna tshogs kyi sgra 'byin cing yid du 'ong ba'i dbyangs rjes su grags pa/ srog gi 'dre
61b8(mdo): ba'i rgyan gyis rnam par brgyan pa/ gang dag gis 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba khrag khrig stong phrag brgyad ngag kun nas yongs su khyebs par byas te//
62a1(mdo): 'gro ba thams cad dga' ba dang / le tog dang sdong po yongs su bskyed pa'i phyir char gyi rgyun rin po che rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par mngon par
62a2(mdo): 'bebs pa'i sprin chen po kun nas spang ngo / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang rlung dmar yang lus sna tshogs kyi sprin sems can thams cad dga' bar byed pa//

69b3(mdo): gakhong du chud pas gzhan gyis gtse ba'i mtshan ma mi 'byung zhing / rang bzhin gyis spyong las sbed du med pa'i las gsum yongs su dag pa'i bsrung chen po dran
69b4(mdo): bum tshogs pa'i mi 'jigs pa dang / chos bzung ba yun du mi brjed pa dang / babs dang shes rab mthar phyin pas sems can sgrol zhing dang bston pa dang /
69b5(mdo): dge ba'i bar chad du mi 'gyur ba'i mi 'jigs pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems mnyams shing / theg pa gzhan gyis mi byung bar nga rang yongs
69b6(mdo): rdzogs pa dang / sems can gyi don rnams pa thams cad du yang dag par thob par bya ba la mi 'jigs pa ste/ bzhi po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa'i mi 'dzi/

70a2(mdo): pa rnams dang / yongs su bsngo ba'i cho gshes pa rnams dang / thabs mkhas pas sems can thams cad kyi sbyong ba'i dbang gis thegs pa'i mchog gis 'byung ba
70a3(mdo): ston pa rnams dang / theg pa chen po las ma nyams pa rnams dang / 'khor ba dang myan las 'das pa'i sgo ston pa rnams dang / gzung dang / snrel ni rgyud la mkha
70a4(mdo): pa rnams dang / ye shes sngon du 'gro bas mngon par 'du mi byed cing / kha na ma tho ba med par che rabs thams cad du mngon du zhugs pa rnams dang / lus
70a5(mdo): dang / ngag dag dang / yid kyi las kyi mtha' dge ba bcu dang ldan pa rnams dang / sdug bsngal gyi phung po thams cad bzod pa'i lus len pas sems can
70a6(mdo): gyi khams thams cad yongs su mi gtong ba rnams dang / 'gro ba thams cad mngon par dga' bar ston pa rnams dang / byis pa dang / nyan thos mi bzang ba

70a8(mdo): chos thams cad kyi thabs sbyin pas/ dbang bskur ba thob par bya ba'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi chos btsal bstan pa las mi ldog pa rnams te/ bco brgyad po de dag ni
70b1(mdo): byang chub sems dpa'i chos mdzes pa rnams so// de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu ga nyen 'di lta ste/ gnas dang / gnasam smin pa'i sangs dang

70b3(mdo): khams sna tshogs mkhyen pa'i stobs dang / dbang po mchog dang / mag ma yin pa mkhyen pa'i sdebs dang / thams cad du 'gro ba'i lam mkhyen pa'i rtsa
